<script>
    var consentKey = "consentSettings";
    var isSiteSponsor = false;
    var consentSettings = {
        pref: false,
        ga: false,
        aa: false,
        ss: isSiteSponsor
    }

    
    function includeGoogleAnalyticsV4() {
        (function(a,b,c,d){
            a=document;b='script';c=a.createElement(b);d=a.createTextNode("var gaIdv4 = 'G-8218P4T90M';");c.appendChild(d);
            a=a.getElementsByTagName(b)[0];a.parentNode.appendChild(c);
        })();
        (function(a,b,c,d){
            a='//www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=G-8218P4T90M';
            b=document;c='script';d=b.createElement(c);d.src=a;d.type='text/java'+c;d.async=true;
            a=b.getElementsByTagName(c)[0];a.parentNode.appendChild(d);
        })();
        (function(a,b,c,d){
            a='/assets/js/ga/analytics.js';
            b=document;c='script';d=b.createElement(c);d.src=a;d.type='text/java'+c;d.async=false;
            a=b.getElementsByTagName(c)[0];a.parentNode.appendChild(d);
        })();
        const userId = ""
        const options = { 'signed_in_status': userId?.length ? "signed_in" : "signed_out" }
        if (userId) {
            options.user_id = userId
        }
        window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
        function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}
        gtag('js', new Date());
        gtag('config', 'G-8218P4T90M', options);
        console.log("GAv4 Loaded");
    }

    function getCookie(cname) {
        var cookie = document.cookie.split("; ").find(c => c.split("=")[0] === cname);
        return cookie ? cookie.split("=")[1] : "";
    }

    function setCookie(cname,cvalue,exdays,cpath)
    {
        var expires = "";
        var path = `path= ${(cpath && cpath.length > 0 ? cpath : "/")};`;
        var domain = `domain=.${location.hostname.replace(/^(www|en|es|it|sv|fr|fr-ca|pt|nl|sv|de|ja)\./i, "")};`;
        if(exdays) {
            let d = new Date();
            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
            expires = `expires=${d.toUTCString()};`;
        }
        document.cookie = `${cname}=${cvalue};${expires}${path}${domain}SameSite=Lax;Secure;`;
    }

    function removeCookie(cname) {
        var expires = `expires=${new Date(0)};`;
        var path = "path=/;";
        var currentPath = `path=${location.pathname};`
        var domain = `domain=.${location.hostname.replace(/^(www|en|es|it|sv|fr|fr-ca|pt|nl|sv|de|ja)\./i, "")};`;
        document.cookie = `${cname}=;${expires}${path}`;
        document.cookie = `${cname}=;${expires}${path}${domain}`;
        document.cookie = `${cname}=;${expires}${currentPath}${domain}`;
    }

    function clearPreferrenceCookies() {
        var preferenceCookies = ["preferredLanguage","tzo","fullSearch","ipLoc","contributorId","email","photoRequestCount","editRequestCount","photosToTranscribeCount","contributeCount","theme","ansub","fileName","currentView","overrideLanguage","fin-ecp","nohvl"];
        var cookies = document.cookie.split("; ");
        cookies.forEach( function(cookie) {
            var cookieKey = cookie.trim().split("=")[0];
            if(preferenceCookies.includes(cookieKey)) {
                removeCookie(cookieKey);
            }
        });
    }

    function isJsonString(str) {
        try {
            JSON.parse(str);
        } catch (e) {
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }
    function googleAnalyticsCheck(vendorConsents, data) {
        if( data && data.gdprApplies){
            if(vendorConsents.consentedVendors.length > 0 && vendorConsents.consentedVendors.find(x=>x.name === "Google Analytics")) {
                consentSettings.ga = true;
                setCookie(consentKey, JSON.stringify(consentSettings));
                includeGoogleAnalyticsV4();
            }
            else {
                consentSettings.ga = false;
                setCookie(consentKey, JSON.stringify(consentSettings));
                console.log("GoogleAnalytics not enabled based on consent.")
            }
        }
        else {
            consentSettings.ga = true;
            setCookie(consentKey, JSON.stringify(consentSettings));
            includeGoogleAnalyticsV4();
        }
    }

    function preferencesCheck(vendorConsents, data) {
        if(data && data.gdprApplies){
            if(vendorConsents.consentedVendors.length > 0 && vendorConsents.consentedVendors.find(x=>x.name === "Ancestry")) {
                consentSettings.pref = true;
                setCookie(consentKey, JSON.stringify(consentSettings));
            }
            else {
                consentSettings.pref = false;
                setCookie(consentKey, JSON.stringify(consentSettings));
                clearPreferrenceCookies();
                console.log("Preferrence cookies not enabled based on consent.")
            }
        }
        else {
            consentSettings.pref = true;
            setCookie(consentKey, JSON.stringify(consentSettings));
        }
    }
    function gdprConsentCheck() {
        var consentValue = getCookie(consentKey);
        if(!isJsonString(consentValue)) {
            __tcfapi('getCustomVendorConsents', 2, function(vendorConsents,success) {
                if(success){
                    //do something for success
                    console.log("getCustomVendorConsents succeeded.");
                    //console.log(vendorConsents);
                    window.__tcfapi('getTCData',2,function(data,success) {
                        googleAnalyticsCheck(vendorConsents, data);
                        preferencesCheck(vendorConsents, data);
                    });
                }
                else{
                    console.log("getCustomVendorConsents failed.");
                }
            });
        }
        else {
            consentSettings = JSON.parse(consentValue);
            if(consentSettings.ga) {includeGoogleAnalyticsV4();}
        }
        $(document).trigger("consent");
    }
</script>

                    <li>Search for an exact birth/death year or select a range, before or after.</li>
                    <li>Select "More search options" to:
                        <ul>
                            <li>Search for a memorial or contributor by <b>ID</b>.</li>
                            <li>Include the name of a <b>spouse, parent, child or sibling</b> in your search.</li>
                            <li>Use partial name search or similar name spellings to catch alternate spellings or broaden your search.</li>
                            <li>Narrow your results to famous, Non-Cemetery Burials, memorials with or without grave photos and more.</li>

<script>
	var currentLocal = "en";
	function setCookie(cname,cvalue,exdays,cpath){
		var expires = "";
		var path = `path= ${(cpath && cpath.length > 0 ? cpath : "/")};`;
		var domain = `domain=.${location.hostname.replace(/^(www|en|es|it|sv|fr|fr-ca|pt|nl|sv|de|ja|ach)\./i, "")};`;
		if(exdays) {
			let d = new Date();
			d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
			expires = `expires=${d.toUTCString()};`;
		}
		document.cookie = `${cname}=${cvalue};${expires}${path}${domain}SameSite=Lax;Secure;`;
	}
	function changeLanguage(locale){
		if (currentLocal !== locale) {
			if (locale === "en") {
				locale = "www";
			}
			if (currentLocal === "en") {
				currentLocal = "www";
			}
			var url = window.location.href;
			if (url.indexOf("?") > 0) {
				url = url + "&overrideLanguage=true";
			}
			else {
				url = url + "?overrideLanguage=true";
			}
			var hash = "#translation-message";
			setCookie("overrideLanguage", locale);
			if (!window.location.hash) {
				url = url.replace(currentLocal, locale) + hash;
			}
			else {
				url = url.replace(currentLocal, locale).replace(window.location.hash, "") + hash;
			}
			window.location.href = url;

		}
	}
</script>

<script>
    var isLive = false;
    var turnstileSiteKey = "0x4AAAAAAAkTWd1yC-DxgQn5";
    var locale = "en";
    var viewIdCaptcha = "memorial-list";
    var memContrib = "";
    var contrib = "";
    var assumedLanguage = false;
    var tp = {
        token: "",
        onload: ""
    };
    $(function() {
      document.cookie = "tzo=" + (-1 * new Date().getTimezoneOffset()) + "; path=/; sameSite=Lax; Secure; domain=." +
        location.hostname.split('.').reverse()[1] + "." +
        location.hostname.split('.').reverse()[0] + ";";
        $(".goto-page").on("keypress", goToPage);
        $("#goto-button").on("click", goToPage);

        if (assumedLanguage) {
            $("#modal-assumed-language").modal('show');
        }

        if (window.location.hash && window.location.hash.substring(1) == "translation-message") {
            $("#modal-translation-message").modal('show');
            history.replaceState("", document.title, window.location.pathname);
        }
        $(".setPreferredLanguage").on("click", function () {
            var locale = $(this).attr("data-locale");
            var expires = new Date(new Date().setFullYear(new Date().getFullYear() + 1));
            document.cookie = "preferredLanguage=" + locale + "; path=/; expires=" + expires + "; domain=." +
                location.hostname.split('.').reverse()[1] + "." +
                location.hostname.split('.').reverse()[0] + ";";
            location.reload();
        })
        $("#updatePreferredLanguage").on("click", function () {
            $("#translationMessageUpdateFailed").addClass("hidden");
            $("#updatePreferredLanguage").attr("disabled", "disabled");
            var locale = $(this).attr("data-locale");
            if (locale == "fr-ca") {
                locale == "fr-CA";
            }
            $.ajax({
                url: "/user/update-preferred-language",
                method: "POST",
                data: {
                    ajax: true,
                    locale: locale
                },
                success: function (result) {

                    document.cookie = "overrideLanguage=; path=/; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; domain=." +
                        location.hostname.split('.').reverse()[1] + "." +
                        location.hostname.split('.').reverse()[0] + ";";
                    var expires = new Date(new Date().setFullYear(new Date().getFullYear() + 1));
                    document.cookie = "preferredLanguage=" + locale + "; path=/; expires=" + expires + "; domain=." +
                        location.hostname.split('.').reverse()[1] + "." +
                        location.hostname.split('.').reverse()[0] + ";";
                    $("#translationMessageUpdated").removeClass("hidden");
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        $("#updatePreferredLanguage").prop("disabled", false);
                        $("#modal-translation-message").modal('hide');
                         $("#translationMessageUpdated").addClass("hidden");
                    }, 1500);
                },
                error: function () {
                    $("#updatePreferredLanguage").prop("disabled", false);
                    $("#translationMessageUpdateFailed").removeClass("hidden");
                }
            });
        });
        $(".declineUpdatePreferredLanguage").on("click", function () {
            $("#modal-translation-message").modal('hide');
        });
        $(".closeTranslationMessageModal").on("click", function() {
            document.cookie = "overrideLanguage=; path=/; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; domain=." +
                location.hostname.split('.').reverse()[1] + "." +
                location.hostname.split('.').reverse()[0] + ";";
            $("#modal-translation-message").modal('hide');
        });
        
    });

    function goToPage(e){
        e.stopPropagation();
        $(".goto-page").removeClass("show-error");
        if((e.type == "keypress" && e.which == 13) || e.type == "click" ){
            e.preventDefault();
            var totalPages = Math.ceil(findagrave.total / findagrave.limit);
            var maxPages = Math.min(totalPages, 500);
            var page = $(".goto-page").val();
            if (page && !isNaN(page) && page > 0 && page <= maxPages){
                const searchUrl = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search.replace(/#\w*/g, ""));
                searchUrl.set("page", page);
                window.location.href = `${window.location.pathname}?${searchUrl.toString().replace(/%23/g, "#")}`;
            }
            else {
                $(".goto-page").addClass("show-error");
            }
        }
    }

    function backToTop(hash){
            if ($(".list-item-page[data-url='page=1']").length > 0){
                $("HTML, BODY").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 700);
            }
            else {
                var searchUrl = window.location.search.replace(/[&?]page=\d+/g, "").replace(/#\w*/g, "");
                var pageString = "";
                if (searchUrl){
                    pageString = searchUrl + "&page=1";
                }
                else {
                    pageString = "?page=1";
                }
                if (hash) {
                    pageString += hash;
                }
                window.location.href = window.location.pathname + pageString;
            }

        }
</script>
